act scene


enter friar tuck

friar holla holla holla follow follow follow
like nois within

now benedicit
what foul absurd
folli fooleri
had like follow
mate
like addlep
invit great state
To see last play
are hunt hay
with Ho way
the goodli hart ran
with follow littl john
much play man
and like sot
have wholli forgot
the cours plot
but crossbow lie
come friar gown
hood cover crown
and low beck
prevent sharp check

blith sit ye wink rude cri
mind left sherwood merrili
the king train robin yeomen tall
gone wood see fat deer fall
We left maid marian busi bower
and pretti jenni look everi hour
for return huntinggam
and therefor seek set thing frame
warman woful sin left
sir doncast whose villani theft
you never heard soon ye shall
hous prior shame befal

the prologu


the proverb how mani men mani minds
which maketh proof hard thing
Of sundri mind pleas sundri kind
In respect infer
that men mind appear differ
No play part alik content

the grave divin call divin
the civil student philosophi
the courtier crave rare sound histori
the baser sort knack pleasantri
So everi sort desireth special
what thing may best content fantasi

but none barren toy afford
To pulpit refer divin
and matter estat council board
As quirk sage philosophi
Or point squirrilit scurril
the one shun childish year rare
thother unfit present

but bring serv time
poor devic pass day withal
To loftier point skill dare climb
lest perk overhigh shame fall
such doth best beseem
such present crave courtesi

that courtesi gentl
which wont pardon fault
which grant requir
your favour desir

the end OF the prologu

scene


enter liber

lib the man virtuou deal doth inur
the less worldli busi molest sure
which maketh proof turmoil still toss worldli mind
So mind exempt worldli toil desir quiet find
and chiefli life led virtuou exercis
there toil eas content wise
but account slight regard virtu
By action worldli stage plainli doth appear
men see without desert virtu nought got
To fortun therefor fli still giveth lot
and find fortun gift pleasant sweet savouri
they build thereon endur perpetu
but sure sure fortun unsur
herself frail gift frail subject everi shower
and end buildeth upon sureti
shall find cast headlong depth miseri
then felt crafti sleight fortun fickl train
Is forc d seek virtu aid reliev
thi end run list man forc must
unless life clean cut man must come unto
In time therefor man might well care estat
lest let extrem repent come late

act I scene


A place provid devil consistori enter
ST dunstan with bead book crosierstaff c

st dun envi alway wait virtu train
and tear grave quiet sleep soul
hath brought mani hundr year
To show upon earth
know list english born
My name dunstan whilst liv d men
chief primat holi english church
begotten west saxoni
My father name heorstan mother cinifr
endow merit legaci
flourish d reign seven great king
the first athelstan whose niec elfleda
malici tongu report defil
next came edmond edr edwi
and reign d edgar great princ
but full mani crime restrain d
edward son lastli ethelr
with king high esteem
and kept land awe
and liv d dane never boast
their begin conquest land
yet accus conjuror
By reason mani miracl
which heaven holi life endow
but whoso look golden legend
that sacr regist holi saint
shall find pope canonis
and happili caus report
might rise reason vision
which beheld great king edgar day
be time abbot glastonburi
which matter worth
make known day
but purpos world shall see
how much slander wrong
nor troubl court king
Or drive feign battl breath
Or keep coil upon stage
but think see secret cell
arm d portass bid bead
but sudden m oercom sleep
If aught ensu watch dunstan dream

he layeth sleep lightn thunder
curtain drawn sudden pluto mino aeacu
rhadamanthu set counsel them malbecco S
ghost guard furies

plu you everdread judg black hell
grim mino aeacu rhadamanth
lord cocytu styx phlegethon
princ dark pluto minist
know great present caus
hath made person sit judg
To hear tharraign malbecco ghost
stand forth thou ghastli pattern despair
and power synod tell thi tale
that may hear thou canst justli say
thou wert author thi decay

mal infern jove great princ tartari
with humbl rever poor malbecco speak
still trembl fatal memori
Of late conclud tragedi
thank great bounti bred
wealthi lord whilst liv d earth
and might continu d day
had plagu mankind fall n
for poor man join d woe unto name
By choos woman wife
wife curs ordain world
fair helena fair inde
but foulli stain d inward wicked
kept brave lov d dear
but dear love cost life
To reckon thousand prank
her pride wast spend unkind
her fals dissembl seem sanctiti
her scold pout prate meddl
and twenti hundr stamp
were heap endless catalogu
Of world plagu d everi day
but main tell
It chanc thu late raini night
crew gallant came unto hous
and nill would forsooth lodg d
brought made good cheer
such store lodg d soft
amongst one yclepe paridel
the falsest thief ever trod ground
robb d stole away wife
lov d dear pursu d thief
and mani day travel spent
found amongst crew satyr wild
kiss coll livelong night
spake fair pray d return
but scorn command gone
and glad fli save life
but backward came unto hous
find spoil d treasur gone
desprat mad ran knew whither
call cri heaven fate
till see none piti distress
threw headlong rock
and conclud ill
now judg justic bencher wife
were instrument end life

plu can possibl lord hell
malbecco tale women true
Is marriag becom great curs
that whilom comfort world

min women seem lost nativ shame
As man better may complain
though made wife
but daughter procur fall

aeac T strang plaint brought us everi day
Of men made miser marriag
So amongst thousand scarc ten
have grievou action gainst wive

rha My lord rhadamanth might counsel
your grace send one world
that might make proof true

plu and wise hast thou counsel rhadamanth
call belphegor present
one furi goe for belphegor
He fittest know hell
To undertak task import
for patient mild piti
humour ill agre kingdom

enter belphegor

and come belphegor
We aw synod decre
upon occas best known
that thou henc shall go world
and take upon thee shape man
In estat thou shalt marri
choos thee wife best may pleas thyself
and live twelvemonth day
thou shalt subject unto human chanc
So far common wit reliev thee
thou shalt us receiv ten thousand pound
suffici stock use thi increas
but whatsoev happen time
look us succour relief
thi shalt thou time expir
bring word us thou hast seen done

bel with heart lord content
So may servant akercock
To wait man
that may wit likewis done

plu We content shall go thee

min but meantim decre majesti
Of poor malbecco

plu He shall rest us
until belphegor return
and find give doom
come let us go set spyal forth
who time must make experi
If hell earth well

exeunt

it thunder lighten devil go forth
dunstan rise runneth stage lay
staff

ST dun satan avaunt thou art man enemi
thou shalt live amongst us unseen
So betray us princ dark
satan avaunt conjur thee hence
what dreamst thou dunstan yea dream d inde

such belik infern king decre
well dunstan content

scene


enter morgan earl london laci earl kent
with mile forrest

mor My lord kent honour know mind
that ever still honour
account daughter happi
amidst infel
that vouchsaf love
how gladli would grant lordship suit
the heaven wit ruthless ear
have often heard yet unpiti plaint
and could find mean recoveri
none wife

sinc laci first suitor daughter
the fairest honorea whose eye
honour love sweet bosom lie
what shall say seem strive heaven
who speechless sent first world
In vain us think loos
that natur self see bound
her beauti virtu join d
are gift suffici though want tongu
and count virtu woman
still bound unoffend silenc
though could wish half land
that could speak sinc may

for have heard lord wondrou fame
Of holi dunstan abbot glastonburi

and rood dovercourt speak
confirm opinion true
and holi consistori fell

that angel often use talk
